Method: 提出TRIP-RAG动态匿名化框架，基于上下文感知的实体量化，从边际隐私风险、知识差异和主题相关性三个维度评估实体，识别高敏感实体并在效用和隐私之间进行权衡。

Result: TRIP-RAG能有效降低上下文推断风险。在保持与完全匿名化相当的隐私保护水平下，Recall@k相比原始数据下降少于35%，生成质量比现有基线提升高达56%。

Conclusion: TRIP-RAG为可变强度的隐私保护场景提供了可行方案，能够在保护隐私的同时显著提升LLM的实用性，解决了现有方法"一刀切"处理敏感实体导致效用严重下降的问题。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enhances the utility of Large Language Models (LLMs) by retrieving external documents. Since the knowledge databases in RAG are predominantly utilized via cloud services, private data in sensitive domains such as finance and healthcare faces the risk of personal information leakage. Thus, effectively anonymizing knowledge bases is crucial for privacy preservation. Existing studies equate the privacy risk of text to the linear superposition of the privacy risks of individual, isolated sensitive entities. The "one-size-fits-all" full processing of all sensitive entities severely degrades utility of LLM. To address this issue, we introduce a dynamic anonymization framework named TRIP-RAG. Based on context-aware entity quantification, this framework evaluates entities from the perspectives of marginal privacy risk, knowledge divergence, and topical relevance. It identifies highly sensitive entities while trading off utility, providing a feasible approach for variable-intensity privacy protection scenarios. Our theoretical analysis and experiments indicate that TRIP-RAG can effectively reduce context inference risks. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that, while maintaining privacy protection comparable to full anonymization, TRIP-RAG's Recall@k decreases by less than 35% compared to the original data, and the generation quality improves by up to 56% over existing baselines.

### [138] [ROAST: Risk-aware Outlier-exposure for Adversarial Selective Training of Anomaly Detectors Against Evasion Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26093)
*Mohammed Elnawawy,Gargi Mitra,Shahrear Iqbal,Karthik Pattabiraman*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: ROAST是一种风险感知的离群点暴露选择性训练框架，通过识别不易受攻击的患者并专注于这些更干净的数据进行训练，提高异常检测器的召回率而不牺牲精确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 医疗等安全关键领域依赖DNN进行预测，但DNN容易受到规避攻击。传统异常检测器对所有患者的良性数据进行无差别训练，忽略了生理差异引入的噪声，降低了鲁棒性和召回率。

Method: 提出ROAST框架：1) 识别不易受攻击的患者；2) 专注于这些更干净、更可靠的数据进行训练；3) 通过向不易受攻击患者的训练集中注入对抗样本来应用离群点暴露，避免使用其他患者的噪声数据。

Result: 实验表明，与无差别训练相比，ROAST平均提高召回率16.2%，减少训练时间88.3%，同时对精确度影响最小。

Conclusion: ROAST框架通过选择性训练和风险感知的离群点暴露，有效提高了异常检测器的召回率，同时保持了精确度，显著减少了训练时间，为安全关键领域的DNN保护提供了更有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Safety-critical domains like healthcare rely on deep neural networks (DNNs) for prediction, yet DNNs remain vulnerable to evasion attacks. Anomaly detectors (ADs) are widely used to protect DNNs, but conventional ADs are trained indiscriminately on benign data from all patients, overlooking physiological differences that introduce noise, degrade robustness, and reduce recall. In this paper, we propose ROAST, a novel risk-aware outlier exposure selective training framework that improves AD recall without sacrificing precision. ROAST identifies patients who are less vulnerable to attack and focuses training on these cleaner, more reliable data, thereby reducing false negatives and improving recall. To preserve precision, the framework applies outlier exposure by injecting adversarial samples into the training set of the less vulnerable patients, avoiding noisy data from others. Experiments show that ROAST increases recall by 16.2\% while reducing the training time by 88.3\% on average compared to indiscriminate training, with minimal impact on precision.

</details>

Conclusion: 该方法适用于云计算和分布式环境中的隐私保护图查询应用，能够有效解决大规模加密图数据查询中的效率和可扩展性问题。

Abstract: With the explosive growth of graph-structured data, graph databases have become a critical infrastructure for supporting large-scale and complex data analysis. Among various graph operations, shortest distance queries play a fundamental role in numerous applications, such as path planning, recommendation systems, and knowledge graphs. However, existing encrypted graph query methods still suffer from limitations in computational efficiency and system scalability, making it challenging to support efficient query processing over large-scale encrypted graph data. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a tensor-based shortest distance query scheme for encrypted graph databases. The proposed method integrates an encrypted 2-hop cover indexing framework with the Pruned Landmark Labeling (PLL) technique, thereby constructing an efficient and privacy-preserving indexing mechanism. Furthermore, a tensorized representation is introduced to uniformly model graph structures, which effectively reduces computational complexity while ensuring data privacy, and significantly improves the scalability of the system. Extensive experimental evaluations on large-scale graph datasets demonstrate that the proposed approach achieves superior scalability and lower computational costs compared with existing encrypted graph query methods. Moreover, it provides strong privacy protection guarantees, making it well suited for privacy-preserving graph query applications in cloud computing and distributed environments.

### [140] [Clawed and Dangerous: Can We Trust Open Agentic Systems?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26221)
*Shiping Chen,Qin Wang,Guangsheng Yu,Xu Wang,Liming Zhu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文系统分析了开放智能体系统的安全挑战，提出了六维分析分类法，综合了50篇相关研究，建立了安全构建智能体平台的参考原则和评估记分卡，指出了当前研究的不足和未来工程议程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放智能体系统（如编码助手、浏览器副驾驶、企业自动化工具）结合了LLM规划、外部能力、持久记忆和特权执行，但其安全挑战与传统软件有根本不同。这些系统的计划生成、决策制定、执行环境都具有概率性特征，核心挑战是在持续不确定性下治理智能体行为，而不仅仅是防御个别攻击。

Method: 通过软件工程视角系统化该领域，引入六维分析分类法，综合分析了50篇涵盖攻击、基准测试、防御、审计和相邻工程基础的论文。基于此综合，提出了安全构建智能体平台的参考原则，并开发了评估平台安全态势的记分卡。

Result: 文献综述显示，当前研究在攻击特征描述和基准构建方面相对成熟，但在部署控制、操作治理、持久记忆完整性和能力撤销方面仍然薄弱。这些差距定义了构建可治理、可审计、在妥协下具有韧性的智能体生态系统的具体工程议程。

Conclusion: 开放智能体系统的安全挑战需要新的治理框架，论文提出的分类法、参考原则和评估工具为构建安全智能体平台提供了系统化方法，指出了未来研究的关键方向，特别是部署控制、操作治理和记忆完整性等薄弱环节。

Abstract: Open agentic systems combine LLM-based planning with external capabilities, persistent memory, and privileged execution. They are used in coding assistants, browser copilots, and enterprise automation. OpenClaw is a visible instance of this broader class.
  Without much attention yet, their security challenge is fundamentally different from that of traditional software that relies on predictable execution and well-defined control flow. In open agentic systems, everything is ''probabilistic'': plans are generated at runtime, key decisions may be shaped by untrusted natural-language inputs and tool outputs, execution unfolds in uncertain environments, and actions are taken under authority delegated by human users. The central challenge is therefore not merely robustness against individual attacks, but the governance of agentic behavior under persistent uncertainty.
  This paper systematizes the area through a software engineering lens. We introduce a six-dimensional analytical taxonomy and synthesize 50 papers spanning attacks, benchmarks, defenses, audits, and adjacent engineering foundations. From this synthesis, we derive a reference doctrine for secure-by-construction agent platforms, together with an evaluation scorecard for assessing platform security posture. Our review shows that the literature is relatively mature in attack characterization and benchmark construction, but remains weak in deployment controls, operational governance, persistent-memory integrity, and capability revocation. These gaps define a concrete engineering agenda for building agent ecosystems that are governable, auditable, and resilient under compromise.

</details>


### [141] [Knowdit: Agentic Smart Contract Vulnerability Detection with Auditing Knowledge Summarization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26270)
*Ziqiao Kong,Wanxu Xia,Chong Wang,Yi Lu,Pan Li,Shaohua Li,Zong Cao,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: Knowdit是一个基于知识图谱和多智能体框架的智能合约漏洞检测系统，通过从历史审计报告中提取DeFi语义知识，实现了对项目特定业务逻辑漏洞的高效检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前DeFi智能合约管理着数十亿美元资产，但自动化漏洞检测面临挑战，因为许多漏洞与项目特定的业务逻辑紧密耦合。研究发现跨不同DeFi业务模型的重复漏洞往往共享相同的底层经济机制（DeFi语义），捕捉这些共享抽象可以实现更系统的审计。

Method: Knowdit首先从历史人工审计报告构建审计知识图谱，将细粒度的DeFi语义与重复漏洞模式关联。对于新项目，采用多智能体框架，通过规范生成、测试工具合成、模糊执行和发现反馈的迭代循环，利用共享工作内存进行持续优化。

Result: 在12个Code4rena项目的75个真实漏洞评估中，Knowdit检测出所有14个高危漏洞和77%的中危漏洞，仅产生2个误报，显著优于所有基线方法。应用于6个真实项目时，进一步发现了12个高危和10个中危的先前未知漏洞。

Conclusion: Knowdit通过知识驱动的方法有效捕捉DeFi语义，实现了对智能合约漏洞的高效检测，在实际应用中表现出色，能够发现先前未知的漏洞，证明了其卓越性能。

Abstract: Smart contracts govern billions of dollars in decentralized finance (DeFi), yet automated vulnerability detection remains challenging because many vulnerabilities are tightly coupled with project-specific business logic. We observe that recurring vulnerabilities across diverse DeFi business models often share the same underlying economic mechanisms, which we term DeFi semantics, and that capturing these shared abstractions can enable more systematic auditing. Building on this insight, we propose Knowdit, a knowledge-driven, agentic framework for smart contract vulnerability detection. Knowdit first constructs an auditing knowledge graph from historical human audit reports, linking fine-grained DeFi semantics with recurring vulnerability patterns. Given a new project, a multi-agent framework leverages this knowledge through an iterative loop of specification generation, harness synthesis, fuzz execution, and finding reflection, driven by a shared working memory for continuous refinement.
  We evaluate Knowdit on 12 recent Code4rena projects with 75 ground-truth vulnerabilities. Knowdit detects all 14 high-severity and 77\% of medium-severity vulnerabilities with only 2 false positives, significantly outperforming all baselines. Applied to six real-world projects, Knowdit further discovers 12 high- and 10 medium-severity previously unknown vulnerabilities, proving its outstanding performance.

</details>


### [142] [PEB Separation and State Migration: Unmasking the New Frontiers of DeFi AML Evasion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26290)
*Yixin Cao,Xianfeng Cheng,Yijie Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文证明当前基于转账图的反洗钱系统在可组合智能合约生态中失效，因为转账层无法捕捉意图发起者、交易执行者和最终受益者分离的结构机制，以及通过合约状态转移而非显式转账的价值迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前工业反洗钱系统基于转账图监控代币流动，隐含假设经济上有意义的价值迁移已充分编码在转账层连接性中。本文旨在证明这一假设在可组合智能合约生态中根本性崩溃。

Method: 形式化两种破坏转账层归因完整性的结构机制：1) 主体-执行-受益人分离机制；2) 状态中介的价值迁移机制。通过现实案例研究（角色分离限价单执行）和构造性跨池套利模型进行验证。

Result: 证明这些机制使转账层观察既不具备归因完整性，也不具备因果封闭性。扩展转账层追踪能力无法解决结构解耦执行固有的归因模糊性。在模块化组合和开放参与市场中，这些机制具有结构生成性。

Conclusion: 基于启发式的资金流追踪已达到形式化观察边界，需要范式转变：从静态图连接性转向基于执行语义的反洗钱系统，专注于从原子执行逻辑和状态不变量中恢复经济因果关系。

Abstract: Transfer-based anti-money laundering (AML) systems monitor token flows through transaction-graph abstractions, implicitly assuming that economically meaningful value migration is sufficiently encoded in transfer-layer connectivity. In this paper, we demonstrate that this assumption, the bedrock of current industrial forensics, fundamentally collapses in composable smart-contract ecosystems.
  We formalize two structural mechanisms that undermine the completeness of transfer-layer attribution. First, we introduce Principal-Execution-Beneficiary (PEB) separation, where intent originators, transaction executors (e.g., MEV searchers), and ultimate beneficiaries are functionally decoupled. Second, we formalize state-mediated value migration, where economic coupling is enforced through invariant-driven contract state transitions (e.g., AMM reserve rebalancing) rather than explicit transfer continuity.
  Through a real-world case study of role-separated limit order execution and a constructive cross-pool arbitrage model, we prove that these mechanisms render transfer-layer observation neither attribution-complete nor causally closed. We further argue that simply expanding transfer-layer tracing capabilities fails to resolve the underlying attribution ambiguity inherent in structurally decoupled execution. Under modular composition and open participation markets, these mechanisms are structurally generative, implying that heuristic-based flow tracing has reached a formal observational boundary. We advocate for a paradigm shift toward AML based on execution semantics, focusing on the restitution of economic causality from atomic execution logic and state invariants rather than static graph connectivity.

</details>

Method: 采用自民族志分析方法，结合作者作为区块链系统工程师、智能合约审计师和上市公司加密货币公司CTO的实践经验，详细研究代币空投、多重签名智能合约和实时链上报告等具体场景。

Conclusion: 自民族志方法对于理解区块链审计的技术复杂性至关重要，本文提出的框架和方法为审计公司应对加密货币资产的存在、所有权、估值和内部控制验证提供了实用解决方案。

Abstract: Blockchain technology introduces asset types and custody mechanisms that fundamentally break traditional financial auditing paradigms. This paper presents an autoethnographic analysis of cryptoasset auditing challenges, build on top of prior research on a comprehensive framework addressing existence, ownership, valuation, and internal control verification. Drawing from lived experience implementing blockchain systems as an engineer, smart contract auditor, and CTO of a publicly traded cryptoasset firm, we demonstrate how autoethnographic methodology becomes necessary for understanding technical complexities that external analysis cannot capture. Through detailed examination of token airdrops, multi-signature smart contracts, and real-time on-chain reporting, we provide experimental approaches and common scenarios that auditing firms can analyze to address blockchain innovations currently considered technically insurmountable.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出H-Elo，一种基于全同态加密（FHE）的隐私评分系统，允许通过传统评分系统进行安全匹配。构建H-Elo系统，分析其对抗有能力攻击者的安全性，并在基于国际象棋的评分更新场景中进行基准测试。

We propose H-Elo, a Fully Homomorphic Encryption (FHE)-based, private rating system, which allows for secure matchmaking through the use of traditional rating systems. In this work, we provide the construction of H-Elo, analyse the security of it against a capable adversary as well as benchmark our construction in a chess-based rating update scenario. Through our experiments we show that H-Elo can achieve similar accuracy to a plaintext implementation, while keeping rating values private and secure. Additionally, we compare our work to other private matchmaking solutions as well as cover some future directions in the field of private matchmaking. To the best of our knowledge we provide one of the first private and secure rating system-based matchmaking protocols.

*Luana Kurmann,Svenja Lage,Violetta Weger*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用有限环上随机码高概率为自由模的特性，以及查询矩阵在移除目标索引对应行后行空间维度下降的现象

Result: 成功构造攻击，服务器能以高概率在多项式时间内确定用户请求的文件索引

Abstract: In this paper we present an attack on a recently proposed code-based Private Information Retrieval (PIR) scheme. Indeed, the server can retrieve the index of the desired file with high probability in polynomial time. The attack relies on the fact that random codes over finite rings are free with high probability and that the dimension of the rowspan of the query matrix decreases when the rows corresponding to the desired index are removed.

### [146] [Towards Privacy-Preserving Federated Learning using Hybrid Homomorphic Encryption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26417)
*Ivan Costa,Pedro Correia,Ivone Amorim,Eva Maia,Isabel Praça*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 该论文提出两种密钥保护机制（掩蔽和RSA封装）来增强联邦学习中混合同态加密的安全性，防止恶意客户端窃取其他客户端的私密模型更新，同时保持模型准确性和低开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的混合同态加密联邦学习系统使用单一密钥对，假设了过于薄弱的威胁模型。如果客户端行为不当或截获其他客户端的流量，私密更新可能被暴露。需要消除这一弱点，将HHE-FL安全性扩展到包含恶意参与者的对抗性环境中。

Method: 提出了两种密钥保护机制集成到HHE-FL工作流程中：1) 掩蔽机制：客户端密钥在加密前被盲化，服务器随后同态地解除盲化；2) RSA封装机制：同态加密的密钥额外使用服务器的RSA公钥进行封装。两种方法都基于Flower框架实现，使用PASTA/BFV HHE方案。

Result: 在MNIST数据集上对12个客户端进行评估，结果显示两种机制都能保持模型准确性，同时增加的开销极小：掩蔽机制成本可忽略不计，RSA封装仅引入适度的运行时和通信开销。

Conclusion: 通过集成掩蔽和RSA封装两种密钥保护机制，成功增强了混合同态加密联邦学习系统的安全性，使其能够抵御恶意客户端的攻击，同时保持了系统的实用性和效率。

Abstract: Federated Learning (FL) enables collaborative training while keeping sensitive data on clients' devices, but local model updates can still leak private information. Hybrid Homomorphic Encryption (HHE) has recently been applied to FL to mitigate client overhead while preserving privacy. However, existing HHE-FL systems rely on a single homomorphic key pair shared across all clients, which forces them to assume an unrealistically weak threat model: if a client misbehaves or intercepts another's traffic, private updates can be exposed. We eliminate this weakness by integrating two alternative key protection mechanisms into the HHE-FL workflow. The first is masking, where client keys are blinded before homomorphic encryption and later unblinded homomorphically by the server. The second is RSA encapsulation, where homomorphically encrypted keys are additionally wrapped under the server's RSA public key. These countermeasures prevent key misuse by other clients and extend HHE-FL security to adversarial settings with malicious participants. We implement both approaches on top of the Flower framework using the PASTA/BFV HHE scheme and evaluate them on the MNIST dataset with 12 clients. Results show that both mechanisms preserve model accuracy while adding minimal overhead: masking incurs negligible cost, and RSA encapsulation introduces only modest runtime and communication overhead.

</details>


### [147] [Reentrancy Detection in the Age of LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26497)
*Dalila Ressi,Alvise Spanò,Matteo Rizzo,Lorenzo Benetollo,Sabina Rossi*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 论文评估了12种基于形式化方法的工具、10个机器学习模型和9个大语言模型在Solidity 0.8+重入漏洞检测中的可靠性表现，发现LLMs在零样本设置下表现最佳，但现有工具在特定场景下仍存在明显缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重入漏洞是以太坊智能合约中最关键的安全漏洞之一，但现有检测工具和数据集仍反映过时的模式和过时的Solidity版本。需要从可靠性角度评估现代Solidity 0.8+代码上最先进的静态分析器和AI技术的表现。

Method: 构建了两个手动验证的基准测试：包含432个真实世界合约的聚合基准，以及包含143个手工制作的最小工作示例的重入场景数据集。然后评估了12个基于形式化方法的工具、10个机器学习模型和9个大语言模型。

Result: 在聚合基准上，传统工具和ML模型最高达到0.87 F1分数，而最佳LLMs在零样本设置下达到0.96。在RSD上，大多数工具在多个场景中失败，最佳工具F1为0.76，最强模型达到0.82。LLMs总体上优于大多数现有检测器。

Conclusion: 领先的大语言模型在重入漏洞检测方面优于大多数现有检测器，突显了当前重入分析工具在鲁棒性和可维护性方面存在令人担忧的差距。需要更可靠和适应性的检测方法。

Abstract: Reentrancy remains one of the most critical classes of vulnerabilities in Ethereum smart contracts, yet widely used detection tools and datasets continue to reflect outdated patterns and obsolete Solidity versions. This paper adopts a dependability-oriented perspective on reentrancy detection in Solidity 0.8+, assessing how reliably state-of-the-art static analyzers and AI-based techniques operate on modern code by putting them to the test on two fronts. We construct two manually verified benchmarks: an Aggregated Benchmark of 432 real-world contracts, consolidated and relabeled from prior datasets, and a Reentrancy Scenarios Dataset (RSD) of \chadded{143} handcrafted minimal working examples designed to isolate and stress-test individual reentrancy patterns. We then evaluate 12 formal-methods-based tools, 10 machine-learning models, and 9 large language models. On the Aggregated Benchmark, traditional tools and ML models achieve up to 0.87 F1, while the best LLMs reach 0.96 in a zero-shot setting. On the RSD, most tools fail on multiple scenarios, the top performer achieving an F1 of 0.76, whereas the strongest model attains 0.82. Overall, our results indicate that leading LLMs outperform the majority of existing detectors, highlighting concerning gaps in the robustness and maintainability of current reentrancy-analysis tools.

</details>

Abstract: Malware continues to be a predominant operational risk for organizations, especially when obfuscation techniques are used to evade detection. Despite the ongoing efforts in the development of Machine Learning (ML) detection approaches, there is still a lack of feature compatibility in public datasets. This limits generalization when facing distribution shifts, as well as transferability to different datasets. This study evaluates the suitability of different data preprocessing approaches for the detection of Portable Executable (PE) files with ML models. The preprocessing pipeline unifies EMBERv2 (2,381-dim) features datasets, trains paired models under two training setups: EMBER + BODMAS and EMBER + BODMAS + ERMDS. Regarding model evaluation, both EMBER + BODMAS and EMBER + BODMAS + ERMDS models are tested against TRITIUM, INFERNO and SOREL-20M. ERMDS is also used for testing for the EMBER + BODMAS setup.

### [149] [BeSafe-Bench: Unveiling Behavioral Safety Risks of Situated Agents in Functional Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25747)
*Yuxuan Li,Yi Lin,Peng Wang,Shiming Liu,Xuetao Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: BeSafe-Bench (BSB) 是一个用于评估情境化智能体行为安全风险的基准测试，涵盖Web、移动、具身VLM和具身VLA四个领域，通过功能环境暴露智能体在真实任务中的安全风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型多模态模型（LMMs）作为自主决策者部署时存在重大无意识行为安全风险，但缺乏全面的安全基准测试，现有评估依赖低保真环境、模拟API或范围狭窄的任务。

Method: 使用功能环境构建多样化的指令空间，通过九类安全关键风险增强任务，采用基于规则的检查和LLM-as-a-judge推理相结合的混合评估框架来评估真实环境影响。

Result: 评估13个流行智能体发现：即使表现最佳的智能体在完全遵守安全约束的情况下也只能完成不到40%的任务，且强大的任务性能经常与严重的安全违规同时发生。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了在现实世界部署智能体系统之前改进安全对齐的紧迫性，揭示了当前智能体在安全约束下的性能与任务完成能力之间存在显著冲突。

Abstract: The rapid evolution of Large Multimodal Models (LMMs) has enabled agents to perform complex digital and physical tasks, yet their deployment as autonomous decision-makers introduces substantial unintentional behavioral safety risks. However, the absence of a comprehensive safety benchmark remains a major bottleneck, as existing evaluations rely on low-fidelity environments, simulated APIs, or narrowly scoped tasks. To address this gap, we present BeSafe-Bench (BSB), a benchmark for exposing behavioral safety risks of situated agents in functional environments, covering four representative domains: Web, Mobile, Embodied VLM, and Embodied VLA. Using functional environments, we construct a diverse instruction space by augmenting tasks with nine categories of safety-critical risks, and adopt a hybrid evaluation framework that combines rule-based checks with LLM-as-a-judge reasoning to assess real environmental impacts. Evaluating 13 popular agents reveals a concerning trend: even the best-performing agent completes fewer than 40% of tasks while fully adhering to safety constraints, and strong task performance frequently coincides with severe safety violations. These findings underscore the urgent need for improved safety alignment before deploying agentic systems in real-world settings.

</details>


### [150] [AutoB2G: A Large Language Model-Driven Agentic Framework For Automated Building-Grid Co-Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26005)
*Borui Zhang,Nariman Mahdavi,Subbu Sethuvenkatraman,Shuang Ao,Flora Salim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AutoB2G是一个基于自然语言描述的自动化建筑-电网协同仿真框架，利用大语言模型自动生成、执行和迭代优化仿真器，改善电网侧性能指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有建筑仿真环境主要关注建筑侧性能指标，缺乏对电网层面影响的系统评估，且实验流程依赖手动配置和大量编程专业知识，需要自动化解决方案。

Method: 扩展CityLearn V2支持建筑-电网交互，采用基于大语言模型的SOCIA框架自动生成仿真器，构建代码库并组织为有向无环图来指导LLM检索完整可执行路径。

Result: 实验结果表明AutoB2G能够有效实现自动化仿真器实现，协调建筑-电网交互以改善电网侧性能指标。

Conclusion: AutoB2G框架通过自然语言任务描述完成整个仿真工作流程，为建筑-电网协同仿真提供了自动化解决方案，解决了现有仿真环境在电网层面评估和自动化方面的不足。

Abstract: The growing availability of building operational data motivates the use of reinforcement learning (RL), which can learn control policies directly from data and cope with the complexity and uncertainty of large-scale building clusters. However, most existing simulation environments prioritize building-side performance metrics and lack systematic evaluation of grid-level impacts, while their experimental workflows still rely heavily on manual configuration and substantial programming expertise. Therefore, this paper proposes AutoB2G, an automated building-grid co-simulation framework that completes the entire simulation workflow solely based on natural-language task descriptions. The framework extends CityLearn V2 to support Building-to-Grid (B2G) interaction and adopts the large language model (LLM)-based SOCIA (Simulation Orchestration for Computational Intelligence with Agents) framework to automatically generate, execute, and iteratively refine the simulator. As LLMs lack prior knowledge of the implementation context of simulation functions, a codebase covering simulation configurations and functional modules is constructed and organized as a directed acyclic graph (DAG) to explicitly represent module dependencies and execution order, guiding the LLM to retrieve a complete executable path. Experimental results demonstrate that AutoB2G can effectively enable automated simulator implementations, coordinating B2G interactions to improve grid-side performance metrics.

</details>


### [151] [Semi-Automated Knowledge Engineering and Process Mapping for Total Airport Management](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26076)
*Darryl Teo,Adharsha Sam,Chuan Shen Marcus Koh,Rakesh Nagi,Nuno Antunes Ribeiro*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种构建机场运营知识图谱的双阶段融合方法，结合符号知识工程和生成式大语言模型，解决机场运营文档的复杂性和数据孤岛问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机场运营文档因技术术语复杂、法规严格、区域信息专有以及多方利益相关者沟通碎片化而难以管理，数据孤岛和语义不一致阻碍了全面机场管理（TAM）计划的实施。

Method: 采用双阶段融合策略：专家策划的知识工程结构指导LLM提示，促进语义对齐知识三元组的发现；结合概率模型进行知识发现和确定性算法进行源头锚定；评估了局部片段推理与文档级处理的上下文窗口利用效果。

Result: 与先前关于LLM长上下文退化的经验观察相反，文档级处理改善了非线性程序依赖关系的恢复；提出的框架确保了绝对可追溯性和可验证性，弥合了生成式输出的"黑盒"特性与操作工具所需的透明度之间的差距。

Conclusion: 该框架通过融合符号知识工程和生成式大语言模型，能够从非结构化文本语料库中合成复杂的操作工作流程，为机场运营知识图谱构建提供了高保真、可追溯的解决方案。

Abstract: Documentation of airport operations is inherently complex due to extensive technical terminology, rigorous regulations, proprietary regional information, and fragmented communication across multiple stakeholders. The resulting data silos and semantic inconsistencies present a significant impediment to the Total Airport Management (TAM) initiative. This paper presents a methodological framework for constructing a domain-grounded, machine-readable Knowledge Graph (KG) through a dual-stage fusion of symbolic Knowledge Engineering (KE) and generative Large Language Models (LLMs).
  The framework employs a scaffolded fusion strategy in which expert-curated KE structures guide LLM prompts to facilitate the discovery of semantically aligned knowledge triples. We evaluate this methodology on the Google LangExtract library and investigate the impact of context window utilization by comparing localized segment-based inference with document-level processing. Contrary to prior empirical observations of long-context degradation in LLMs, document-level processing improves the recovery of non-linear procedural dependencies.
  To ensure the high-fidelity provenance required in airport operations, the proposed framework fuses a probabilistic model for discovery and a deterministic algorithm for anchoring every extraction to its ground source. This ensures absolute traceability and verifiability, bridging the gap between "black-box" generative outputs and the transparency required for operational tooling. Finally, we introduce an automated framework that operationalizes this pipeline to synthesize complex operational workflows from unstructured textual corpora.

### [152] [CADSmith: Multi-Agent CAD Generation with Programmatic Geometric Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26512)
*Jesse Barkley,Rumi Loghmani,Amir Barati Farimani*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CADSmith是一个多智能体文本到CAD生成系统，通过嵌套校正循环和程序化几何验证实现高质量CAD代码生成


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到CAD生成方法要么单次生成无几何验证，要么依赖有损视觉反馈无法解决尺寸错误，需要更精确可靠的解决方案

Method: CADSmith采用多智能体管道，从自然语言生成CadQuery代码，通过内外两层校正循环迭代优化：内循环解决执行错误，外循环基于OpenCASCADE内核的精确测量和视觉语言模型的整体评估进行程序化几何验证

Result: 在100个提示的三级难度基准测试中，相比零样本基线，CADSmith实现100%执行率（从95%提升），中位F1分数从0.9707提升到0.9846，中位IoU从0.8085提升到0.9629，平均Chamfer距离从28.37降低到0.74

Conclusion: 基于程序化几何反馈的闭环精炼显著提高了LLM生成的CAD模型的质量和可靠性，检索增强生成方法避免了微调需求，能适应CAD库的持续演进

Abstract: Existing methods for text-to-CAD generation either operate in a single pass with no geometric verification or rely on lossy visual feedback that cannot resolve dimensional errors. We present CADSmith, a multi-agent pipeline that generates CadQuery code from natural language. It then undergoes an iterative refinement process through two nested correction loops: an inner loop that resolves execution errors and an outer loop grounded in programmatic geometric validation. The outer loop combines exact measurements from the OpenCASCADE kernel (bounding box dimensions, volume, solid validity) with holistic visual assessment from an independent vision-language model Judge. This provides both the numerical precision and the high-level shape awareness needed to converge on the correct geometry. The system uses retrieval-augmented generation over API documentation rather than fine-tuning, maintaining a current database as the underlying CAD library evolves. We evaluate on a custom benchmark of 100 prompts in three difficulty tiers (T1 through T3) with three ablation configurations. Against a zero-shot baseline, CADSmith achieves a 100% execution rate (up from 95%), improves the median F1 score from 0.9707 to 0.9846, the median IoU from 0.8085 to 0.9629, and reduces the mean Chamfer Distance from 28.37 to 0.74, demonstrating that closed-loop refinement with programmatic geometric feedback substantially improves the quality and reliability of LLM-generated CAD models.

</details>


### [153] [Stabilizing Rubric Integration Training via Decoupled Advantage Normalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26535)
*Zelin Tan,Zhouliang Yu,Bohan Lin,Zijie Geng,Hejia Geng,Yudong Zhang,Mulei Zhang,Yang Chen,Shuyue Hu,Zhenfei Yin,Chen Zhang,Lei Bai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PAPO是一种将过程级评估集成到GRPO中的方法，通过解耦优势归一化解决现有奖励设计的两个限制：结果奖励模型只评估最终答案正确性，过程奖励模型容易导致奖励黑客攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有奖励设计存在两个主要问题：结果奖励模型（ORM）只评估最终答案正确性，将所有正确答案同等对待，忽略推理质量，且当所有回答都正确时优势信号逐渐消失；过程奖励模型（PRM）提供更丰富的监督，但直接使用会导致奖励黑客攻击，模型通过冗长回答来提升分数而准确性崩溃。

Method: 提出过程感知策略优化（PAPO），将过程级评估集成到组相对策略优化（GRPO）中，通过解耦优势归一化。优势由两个部分组成：结果组件Aout（来自ORM，在所有响应上归一化）和过程组件Aproc（来自基于规则的PRM，仅在正确响应中归一化）。这种解耦设计确保Aout锚定训练的正确性，而Aproc区分推理质量而不扭曲结果信号。

Result: 在多个模型规模和六个基准测试上的实验表明，PAPO始终优于ORM，在OlympiadBench上达到51.3% vs. 46.3%，并且在ORM达到平台期和下降时继续改进。

Conclusion: PAPO通过解耦优势归一化有效解决了现有奖励设计的局限性，既保持了正确性锚定，又能够区分推理质量，在多个基准测试中表现出持续改进的优势。

Abstract: We propose Process-Aware Policy Optimization (PAPO), a method that integrates process-level evaluation into Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) through decoupled advantage normalization, to address two limitations of existing reward designs. Outcome reward models (ORM) evaluate only final-answer correctness, treating all correct responses identically regardless of reasoning quality, and gradually lose the advantage signal as groups become uniformly correct. Process reward models (PRM) offer richer supervision, but directly using PRM scores causes reward hacking, where models exploit verbosity to inflate scores while accuracy collapses. PAPO resolves both by composing the advantage from an outcome component Aout, derived from ORM and normalized over all responses, and a process component Aproc, derived from a rubric-based PRM and normalized exclusively among correct responses. This decoupled design ensures that Aout anchors training on correctness while Aproc differentiates reasoning quality without distorting the outcome signal. Experiments across multiple model scales and six benchmarks demonstrate that PAPO consistently outperforms ORM, reaching 51.3% vs.\ 46.3% on OlympiadBench while continuing to improve as ORM plateaus and declines.

</details>

Method: 与IREB AI & RE特别兴趣小组合作，对RE从业者进行调查，采用定量和定性数据分析方法，研究生成式AI在需求获取、分析、规格说明、验证和管理中的应用。

Abstract: Context and motivation: With the rapid advancement of AI technologies, there is an increasing need to understand how AI can be effectively integrated into RE processes. In recent years, several studies have explored the potential and challenges of applying GenAI to support or even automate RE-related activities. Question/problem: Despite the existing body of knowledge on AI's potential for supporting RE activities, there is limited evidence on its practical applicability and limitations from an industry perspective. Principal ideas/results: To address this gap, we conducted a survey with RE practitioners in collaboration with the IREB Special Interest Group on AI & RE. In addition to describing our research methodology and survey design, we present insights from our quantitative and qualitative data analyzes. These insights include practitioners' perspectives on current usage scenarios, concerns, experiences-both positive and negative-as well as training needs related to using GenAI in requirements elicitation, analysis, specification, validation, and management. Contribution: This study provides empirical evidence on the practical use of GenAI in RE, offering insights into its benefits, challenges, and training needs. The findings inform future research and industry strategies, guiding effective AI integration and skill development for improved RE processes and results.

### [155] [A Large-scale Empirical Study on the Generalizability of Disclosed Java Library Vulnerability Exploits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25997)
*Zirui Chen,Qi Zhan,Jiayuan Zhou,Xing Hu,Xin Xia,Xiaohu Yang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究首次大规模实证分析了漏洞利用代码在Java库版本间的适用性，发现即使不迁移，利用代码也能达到83.0%的召回率和99.3%的精确度识别受影响版本，通过手动迁移可将召回率提升至96.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开源软件供应链安全严重依赖准确评估库漏洞的受影响版本。虽然先前研究已利用漏洞利用代码验证受影响版本，但存在一个关键限制：利用代码通常是版本特定的，不能直接跨版本应用。尽管这一限制被广泛认可，但尚未在大规模范围内进行系统验证，导致利用代码跨版本的实际适用性未被充分探索。

Method: 构建了包含259个利用代码、128个Java库、28,150个历史版本和61个CWE的综合数据集。执行每个利用代码对抗库版本历史，并与手动标注的真实受影响版本进行比较。进一步调查利用代码执行与真实情况不一致的根本原因，并探索利用代码迁移策略。

Result: 1) 即使不迁移，利用代码在Java中识别受影响版本能达到83.0%的召回率和99.3%的精确度，优于大多数广泛使用的漏洞数据库和评估工具。2) 这一能力使研究团队能够为CPE字典贡献796个确认缺失的受影响版本。3) 剩余的利用失败主要源于库演进引入的兼容性问题和变化的环境约束。4) 通过手动迁移1,885个版本的利用代码，并从中提炼出10种策略的分类法，将总体召回率提升至96.1%。

Conclusion: 漏洞利用代码在跨库版本识别受影响版本方面具有很高的实用价值，即使不迁移也能达到良好效果。通过系统迁移策略可以显著提升其覆盖范围。该研究为开源软件供应链安全提供了重要的实证依据，并提出了有效的利用代码迁移方法。

Abstract: Open-source software supply chain security relies heavily on assessing affected versions of library vulnerabilities. While prior studies have leveraged exploits for verifying vulnerability affected versions, they point out a key limitation that exploits are version-specific and cannot be directly applied across library versions. Despite being widely acknowledged, this limitation has not been systematically validated at scale, leaving the actual applicability of exploits across versions unexplored. To fill this gap, we conduct the first large-scale empirical study on exploit applicability across library versions. We construct a comprehensive dataset consisting of 259 exploits spanning 128 Java libraries and 28,150 historical versions, covering 61 CWEs that account for 76.33% of vulnerabilities in Maven. Leveraging this dataset, we execute each exploit against the library version history and compare the execution outcomes with our manually annotated ground-truth affected versions. We further investigate the root causes of inconsistencies between exploit execution and ground truth, and explore strategies for exploit migration. Our results (RQ1) show that, even without migration, exploits achieve 83.0% recall and 99.3% precision in identifying affected versions in Java, outperforming most widely used vulnerability databases and assessment tools. Notably, this capability enables us to contribute 796 confirmed missing affected versions to the CPE dictionary. We investigate the remaining exploit failures (RQ2) and find that they mainly stem from compatibility issues introduced by library evolution and changing environmental constraints. Based on these observations, we manually migrate exploits for 1,885 versions and distill a taxonomy of 10 strategies from these successful adaptation cases (RQ3), thereby increasing the overall recall to 96.1%.

</details>


### [156] [SWE-PRBench: Benchmarking AI Code Review Quality Against Pull Request Feedback](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26130)
*Deepak Kumar*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SWE-PRBench是一个包含350个带人工标注的pull request基准测试，用于评估AI代码审查质量。在验证过的LLM-as-judge框架下，8个前沿模型在仅diff配置中只能检测到15-31%的人工标记问题，表明AI代码审查远低于人类专家水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前AI代码审查能力评估缺乏标准基准，尽管在代码生成基准上表现良好，但实际代码审查质量仍不明确。需要系统评估AI在真实pull request审查中的表现，并分析不同上下文配置对性能的影响。

Method: 从活跃开源仓库中筛选700个候选pull request，使用Repository Quality Score过滤，最终选择350个构建基准。采用三种冻结上下文配置：仅diff、diff加文件内容、完整上下文。使用LLM-as-judge框架（kappa=0.75）评估8个前沿模型，分析上下文策略对问题检测的影响。

Result: 所有8个模型从配置A到配置C性能单调下降，即使通过结构化语义层（AST提取的函数上下文和导入图解析）提供上下文。主要机制是Type2_Contextual问题检测在配置B中崩溃，与长上下文中注意力稀释一致。结构化2000token的diff-with-summary提示优于2500token的完整上下文提示。前四个模型统计上无差异（平均分0.147-0.153），与后四个模型（平均分≤0.113）存在明显差距。

Conclusion: AI代码审查仍远低于人类专家水平，当前模型在长上下文处理中存在注意力稀释问题。结构化简洁提示优于信息丰富的完整上下文，表明需要更有效的上下文管理策略。数据集和评估工具已公开发布。

Abstract: We introduce SWE-PRBench, a benchmark of 350 pull requests with human-annotated ground truth for evaluating AI code review quality. Evaluated against an LLM-as-judge framework validated at kappa=0.75, 8 frontier models detect only 15-31% of human-flagged issues on the diff-only configuration, demonstrating that AI code review remains far below human expert performance despite strong results on code generation benchmarks. Pull requests are drawn from active open-source repositories, filtered from 700 candidates using a Repository Quality Score, and evaluated under three frozen context configurations: diff only (config_A), diff with file content (config_B), and full context (config_C), enabling systematic ablation of context provision strategies. All 8 models degrade monotonically from config_A to config_C, even when context is provided via structured semantic layers including AST-extracted function context and import graph resolution. The dominant mechanism is a collapse of Type2_Contextual issue detection at config_B, consistent with attention dilution in long contexts: a structured 2,000-token diff-with-summary prompt outperforms a 2,500-token full-context prompt enriched with execution context, behaviour mapping, and test signatures across all 8 models. The top four models are statistically indistinguishable (mean score 0.147-0.153) while a clear tier gap separates them from the remaining four (mean score <= 0.113). Dataset, contexts, annotations, and evaluation harness are released publicly.

</details>


### [157] [IncreRTL: Traceability-Guided Incremental RTL Generation under Requirement Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25769)
*Luanrong Chen,Renzhi Chen,Xinyu Li,Shanshan Li,Rui Gong,Lei Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出IncreRTL框架，通过构建需求-代码可追溯性链接来定位和重新生成受影响的代码段，实现增量更新

Result: 在新构建的EvoRTL-Bench基准测试上评估，IncreRTL在重新生成一致性和效率方面表现出显著改进

Conclusion: IncreRTL推动了基于LLM的RTL生成向实际工程部署迈进，能够更有效地处理需求演化

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in generating RTL code from natural-language descriptions, but existing methods remain static and struggle to adapt to evolving design requirements, potentially causing structural drift and costly full regeneration. We propose IncreRTL, a LLM-driven framework for incremental RTL generation under requirement evolution. By constructing requirement-code traceability links to locate and regenerate affected code segments, IncreRTL achieves accurate and consistent updates. Evaluated on our newly constructed EvoRTL-Bench, IncreRTL demonstrates notable improvements in regeneration consistency and efficiency, advancing LLM-based RTL generation toward practical engineering deployment.

</details>


### [158] [From Personas to Programming: Gender-specific Effects of Design Thinking-Based Computing Education at Secondary Schools](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26194)
*Isabella Graßl,Gordon Fraser,Daniela Damian*

Main category: cs.SE

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索设计思维的共情驱动方法是否能解决软件工程领域存在的性别兴趣差距问题，特别是在青少年早期教育阶段。

Method: 采用10周课程整合的设计思维软件开发课程，研究对象为加拿大两所学校的55名13-15岁中学生，通过比较性别差异来评估知识获取、兴趣提升以及社会情感体验的变化。

Result: 结果显示：1）男女学生都获得了软件开发的感知知识；2）女生在自我效能、兴趣、可持续性话题参与度以及幸福感（乐观、有用感、社会连接）方面有显著提升；3）创造性协作阶段产生最积极情绪，技术任务导致一定程度的无聊感（尤其在男生中），但整体仍有收益。

Abstract: Creative approaches to attract students to software engineering at an early age are emerging, yet their differential impact on gender remains unclear. This study investigates whether design thinking's empathy-driven approach addresses the documented gender gap in interest in software engineering. In a 10-week curriculum-integrated design thinking software development course with 55 secondary school students aged 13-15 from two schools in Canada, we examined gendered differences in perceived gains in knowledge and interest, as well as in social-emotional experiences. Our results show that both girls and boys gained perceived knowledge in software development. However, girls showed significant improvements in self-efficacy, interest, engagement with sustainability topics, and well-being, including optimism, sense of usefulness, and social connectedness. Positive emotions were strongest during creative, collaborative phases, while technical tasks led to some boredom, especially among boys, though they still benefited overall. This suggests that human-centred design thinking might be one effective way to address gender equity challenges, though we need more differentiated technical implementations.

</details>


### [159] [An Object Web Seminar: A Retrospective on a Technical Dialogue Still Reverbarating](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26203)
*James J. Cusick*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过分析1999年研讨会内容，探讨了对象技术与早期Web融合的巅峰时期，展示了分布式架构的演变，并论证了这些方法虽名称改变但核心设计原则仍在当今技术中延续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 技术变革迅速，新趋势往往掩盖了昨日的新技术。本文旨在通过分析1999年研讨会内容，重新审视对象技术与早期Web融合的巅峰时期，探索分布式架构的演变，并论证这些历史方法对当今软件世界的持续影响。

Method: 通过分析1999年举办的研讨会内容，探讨对象Web（Object Web）的历史、演变和使用。研究当时的新开发工具、架构设计，并将这些方法与当今流行的技术（如Kubernetes和微服务）进行对比分析。

Result: 研究发现，虽然"对象Web"这一术语已不再流行，但其核心设计属性仍在当今技术中延续。Kubernetes和微服务等现代技术仍然体现了对象Web的核心设计原则。此外，研讨会还展示了四分之一世纪前的早期AI工具，为当前AI技术热潮提供了历史视角。

Conclusion: 技术潮流会变化，但核心设计原则具有持久性。对象Web虽然名称不再流行，但其设计理念仍在现代分布式系统中延续。同时，当前AI技术热潮也需要从历史技术浪潮的视角来审视，避免过度关注短期趋势而忽视长期价值。

Abstract: Technology change happens quickly such that new trends tend to crowd out the focus on what was new just yesterday. In this paper the peak popularity of the confluence of Object Technologies with early Web adoption is explored through the content of a seminar held in 1999. Distributed architectures were undergoing significant change at this point, and deeper software capabilities were just beginning to be broadly accessible over the Internet. The Object Web arose and was infused with new development tools reflecting these capabilities and allowing design of applications for deployment during the early days of the World Wide Web. This conference discussed the history, evolution, and use of these tools, architectures, and their future possibilities. The continued dominance of these approaches although under different names is demonstrated even though the term Object Web has receded in use. Favored newer offerings such as Kubernetes and microservices still model the core design attributes of the Object Web for example. Aside from connecting this seminar to relevance in the software world of today this paper also touches on the early AI tools demonstrated in this seminar a quarter century ago and how the popularity wave of any given technology might affect the current focus on AI technology offerings.

</details>


### [160] [Automating Domain-Driven Design: Experience with a Prompting Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26244)
*Tobias Eisenreich,Husein Jusic,Stefan Wagner*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个基于大语言模型的提示框架，用于自动化领域驱动设计（DDD）的核心活动，通过五个步骤分解DDD流程，在案例研究中验证了框架的有效性，发现前三个步骤效果良好，但后两个步骤因错误累积而效果不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 领域驱动设计（DDD）是构建复杂软件系统的强大设计技术，但实施过程需要大量专家投入。本文旨在通过大语言模型（LLM）自动化DDD的核心活动，减少专家工作量，同时保持以人为中心的决策过程。

Method: 提出了一个提示框架，将DDD分解为五个顺序步骤：1）建立通用语言，2）模拟事件风暴，3）识别限界上下文，4）设计聚合，5）映射到技术架构。在FTAPI企业平台的真实需求案例研究中验证了该框架。

Result: 前三个步骤（建立通用语言、模拟事件风暴、识别限界上下文）能够一致地生成有价值且可用的工件，但后两个步骤（设计聚合、映射到技术架构）由于小错误或不准确性的传播和累积，生成的工件不实用。整体上，框架作为协作伙伴在构建可操作文档方面表现优异，但不能完全自动化。

Conclusion: 大语言模型可以增强但不能替代架构专业知识，提供了一个实用工具来减少DDD的工作量和开销，同时保持以人为中心的决策过程。框架最适合作为协作伙伴生成文档，而不是完全自动化设计过程。

Abstract: Domain-driven design (DDD) is a powerful design technique for architecting complex software systems. This paper introduces a prompting framework that automates core DDD activities through structured large language model (LLM) interactions. We decompose DDD into five sequential steps: (1) establishing an ubiquitous language, (2) simulating event storming, (3) identifying bounded contexts, (4) designing aggregates, and (5) mapping to technical architecture. In a case study, we validated the prompting framework against real-world requirements from FTAPI's enterprise platform. While the first steps consistently generate valuable and usable artifacts, later steps show how minor errors or inaccuracies can propagate and accumulate. Overall, the framework excels as a collaborative sparring partner for building actionable documentation, such as glossaries and context maps, but not for full automation. This allows the experts to concentrate their discussion on the critical trade-offs. In our evaluation, Steps 1 to 3 worked well, but the accumulated errors rendered the artifacts generated from Steps 4 and 5 impractical. Our findings show that LLMs can enhance, but not replace, architectural expertise, offering a practical tool to reduce the effort and overhead of DDD while preserving human-centric decision-making.

</details>


### [161] [Developers and Generative AI: A Study of Self-Admitted Usage in Open Source Projects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26277)
*Rosalia Tufano,Federica Pepe,Fiorella Zampetti,Antonio Mastropaolo,Ozren Dabić,Massimiliano Di Penta,Gabriele Bavota*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究通过挖掘GitHub提交、问题和拉取请求，对ChatGPT和GitHub Copilot在软件开发中的自我承认使用进行了定性调查，创建了包含64个任务的分类法，并分析了两年间的使用变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI工具如ChatGPT和GitHub Copilot正在重塑软件开发方式，开发者在使用这些工具时会在软件制品中留下痕迹。了解AI在软件开发中的使用情况，以及让其他人了解这些软件制品是如何创建的（例如出于许可或可信度目的），具有重要价值。

Method: 通过挖掘GitHub中的提交、问题和拉取请求，寻找ChatGPT和GitHub Copilot的使用痕迹，然后通过人工编码创建分类法。研究重复了两年前的分析并扩展到GitHub Copilot，比较使用途径的变化。

Result: 创建了包含64个不同ChatGPT和GitHub Copilot使用任务的分类法，分为7个类别。研究显示使用途径已经扩展，开发者认为生成式AI使用有用，并且一些一年多前的担忧已不再存在。

Conclusion: 该定性研究得出的任务分类法为开发者提供了关于如何将生成式AI集成到工作流程中的宝贵见解，并为研究人员提供了开发者认为适合自动化的任务的清晰概述。

Abstract: The availability of generative Artificial Intelligence (AI) tools such as ChatGPT or GitHub Copilot is reshaping the way in which software is developed, evolved, and maintained. Oftentimes, developers leave traces of such an usage in software artifacts. This allows not only to understand how AI is used in software development, but also to let others be aware how such software artifacts were created, e.g., for licensing or trustworthiness purposes. This paper-building upon our preliminary work presented at MSR 2024-aims at qualitatively investigating on the self-admitted use of two very popular generative AI tools - ChatGPT and GitHub Copilot - in software development. To this aim, we mined GitHub for such traces, by looking at commits, issues and pull requests (PRs). Then, through a manual coding, we create a taxonomy of 64 different ChatGPT and GitHub Copilot usage tasks, grouped into 7 categories. By repeating our previous analysis two years after and by extending it to GitHub Copilot, we show how the usage avenues have been expanded, the extent to which developers perceived such a generative AI usage useful, and whether some concerns occurring more than one year ago are no longer present. The taxonomy of tasks we derived from such a qualitative study provided (i) developers with valuable insights into how generative AI can be integrated into their workflows, and (ii) researchers with a clear overview of tasks that developers perceive as well-suited for automation.

</details>


### [162] [Beyond Banning AI: A First Look at GenAI Governance in Open Source Software Communities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26487)
*Wenhao Yang,Runzhi He,Minghui Zhou*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析67个高可见度开源项目中关于生成式AI治理的质性材料，识别了贡献工作流中的常见问题，提出了三种治理导向和12种治理策略，为开源社区管理AI辅助贡献提供了系统框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式AI在开源软件中的作用日益重要，但AI生成内容的维护负担促使开源项目制定了各种AI治理规则。目前缺乏统一的治理框架和实践指导，社区应对措施分散，需要系统性的研究来理解和管理AI在开源中的影响。

Method: 采用多阶段分析方法，从67个高可见度开源项目中收集与生成式AI治理相关的各种质性材料，进行系统性分析，识别模式、问题和解决方案。

Result: 研究发现开源社区对生成式AI的治理远不止"禁止与否"的问题，识别了贡献工作流中的常见关切，提出了三种治理导向（责任导向、验证导向、能力导向），并映射出12种治理策略及其实现模式，涵盖了责任归属、验证机制、审查能力、代码来源和平台基础设施等多个维度。

Conclusion: 开源项目中生成式AI的治理需要跨多个维度的协调响应，研究将分散的社区实践提炼为结构化概述，为研究人员提供了概念基础，为维护者和平台设计者提供了实用参考，推动了开源AI治理的系统化理解。

Abstract: Generative AI (GenAI) is playing an increasingly important role in open source software (OSS). Beyond completing code and documentation, GenAI is increasingly involved in issues, pull requests, code reviews, and security reports. Yet, cheaper generation does not mean cheaper review - and the resulting maintenance burden has pushed OSS projects to experiment with GenAI-specific rules in contribution guidelines, security policies, and repository instructions, even including a total ban on AI-assisted contributions. However, governing GenAI in OSS is far more than a ban-or-not question. The responses remain scattered, with neither a shared governance framework in practice nor a systematic understanding in research. Therefore, in this paper, we conduct a multi-stage analysis on various qualitative materials related to GenAI governance retrieved from 67 highly visible OSS projects. Our analysis identifies recurring concerns across contribution workflows, derives three governance orientations, and maps out 12 governance strategies and their implementation patterns. We show that governing GenAI in OSS extends well beyond banning - it requires coordinated responses across accountability, verification, review capacity, code provenance, and platform infrastructure. Overall, our work distills dispersed community practices into a structured overview, providing a conceptual baseline for researchers and a practical reference for maintainers and platform designers.

</details>


### [163] [Sustainability Is Not Linear: Quantifying Performance, Energy, and Privacy Trade-offs in On-Device Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26603)
*Eziyo Ehsani,Luca Giamattei,Ivano Malavolta,Roberto Pietrantuono*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 研究发现大语言模型从云端迁移到边缘设备时面临内存、能耗和性能的权衡，量化技术虽能减少内存占用但节能效果有限，而MoE架构能在保持小模型能耗的同时提供大模型容量，Qwen2.5-3B等中等规模模型在质量与能耗间达到最佳平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型从云端集群迁移到边缘设备虽然能增强隐私保护和离线访问能力，但面临移动设备电池、温度限制和内存约束等物理限制。需要研究在实际用户条件下的能耗、延迟和质量之间的复杂权衡关系。

Method: 构建可重复的实验流水线，在无需root权限的情况下，在三星Galaxy S25 Ultra旗舰Android设备上对8个参数量从0.5B到9B的模型进行细粒度功耗测量，开展实证案例研究，分析量化技术、MoE架构对能耗的影响。

Result: 发现量化-能耗悖论：现代重要性感知量化虽能减少内存占用，但与标准混合精度方法相比节能效果可忽略；MoE架构打破标准尺寸-能耗趋势，7B模型的存储容量仅需1B-2B模型的能耗；Qwen2.5-3B等中等规模模型在响应质量和可持续能耗间达到最佳平衡点。

Conclusion: 对于电池寿命而言，模型架构而非量化方案是决定性因素；MoE架构在边缘设备部署中具有显著优势；中等规模模型在质量与能耗间存在实用最佳平衡点，为边缘设备上的LLM部署提供了重要指导。

Abstract: The migration of Large Language Models (LLMs) from cloud clusters to edge devices promises enhanced privacy and offline accessibility, but this transition encounters a harsh reality: the physical constraints of mobile batteries, thermal limits, and, most importantly, memory constraints. To navigate this landscape, we constructed a reproducible experimental pipeline to profile the complex interplay between energy consumption, latency, and quality. Unlike theoretical studies, we captured granular power metrics across eight models ranging from 0.5B to 9B parameters without requiring root access, ensuring our findings reflect realistic user conditions. We harness this pipeline to conduct an empirical case study on a flagship Android device, the Samsung Galaxy S25 Ultra, establishing foundational hypotheses regarding the trade-offs between generation quality, performance, and resource consumption. Our investigation uncovered a counter-intuitive quantization-energy paradox. While modern importance-aware quantization successfully reduces memory footprints to fit larger models into RAM, we found it yields negligible energy savings compared to standard mixed-precision methods. This proves that for battery life, the architecture of the model, not its quantization scheme, is the decisive factor. We further identified that Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures defy the standard size-energy trend, offering the storage capacity of a 7B model while maintaining the lower energy profile of a 1B to 2B model. Finally, an analysis of these multi-objective trade-offs reveals a pragmatic sweet spot of mid-sized models, such as Qwen2.5-3B, that effectively balance response quality with sustainable energy consumption.

</details>

### [164] [Decentralized Value Systems Agreements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25811)
*Arturo Hernandez-Sanchez,Natalia Criado,Stella Heras,Miguel Rebollo,Jose Such*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 提出一种聚合价值系统的新方法，生成多个价值协议以容纳不同个体间的价值系统差异，相比现有寻找单一协议的方法更适合异质社会。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 价值决策面临主观性挑战：不同个体对价值的相对重要性评估不同，对价值含义的解释也不同。虽然社会成员可能共享某些原则或价值，但他们的价值系统（如何解释这些价值及赋予的相对重要性）存在显著差异。现有方法只寻找单一价值协议，不适合现实的异质社会。

Method: 提出新颖的价值系统聚合方法：1）个体表明其价值系统及愿意让步的程度；2）采用去中心化优化方法寻找一组协议（而非单一协议）；3）应用参与式价值评估过程和欧洲价值观调查的真实数据验证方法。

Result: 在两个真实场景中应用该方法：1）参与式价值评估过程数据；2）欧洲价值观调查数据。结果显示，与现有价值系统聚合技术相比，该方法在个体效用方面有显著改善，能够获得不同的聚合结果。

Conclusion: 该方法通过生成多个价值协议来容纳价值系统间的固有差异，相比寻找单一协议的方法更适合异质社会，在实际应用中显示出个体效用的显著提升。

Abstract: One of the biggest challenges of value-based decision-making is dealing with the subjective nature of values. The relative importance of a value for a particular decision varies between individuals, and people may also have different interpretations of what aligning with a value means in a given situation. While members of a society are likely to share a set of principles or values, their value systems--that is, how they interpret these values and the relative importance they give to them--have been found to differ significantly. This work proposes a novel method for aggregating value systems, generating distinct value agreements that accommodate the inherent differences within these systems. Unlike existing work, which focuses on finding a single value agreement, the proposed approach may be more suitable for a realistic and heterogeneous society. In our solution, the agents indicate their value systems and the extent to which they are willing to concede. Then, a set of agreements is found, taking a decentralized optimization approach. Our work has been applied to identify value agreements in two real-world scenarios using data from a Participatory Value Evaluation process and a European Value Survey. These case studies illustrate the different aggregations that can be obtained with our method and compare them with those obtained using existing value system aggregation techniques. In both cases, the results showed a substantial improvement in individual utilities compared to existing alternatives.

</details>
